<td style="text-align:left">National annual estimate<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">[141]</a></sup></td>
<td>The <a href="/wiki/Political_status_of_Kosovo" title="Political status of Kosovo">political status of Kosovo</a> is disputed. Having unilaterally declared independence from <a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Serbia</a> in 2008, Kosovo <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Kosovo" title="International recognition of Kosovo">is formally recognised as an independent state</a> by 97 UN member states (with another 15 states recognising it at some point but then withdrawing their recognition) and 96 states not recognizing it, while Serbia continues to claim it as part of its own sovereign territory.
</td></tr>

<td style="text-align:right">245,424</td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-size:inherit"><span data-sort-value="6,997,307,810,819,960,000♠" style="display:none"></span>0.00308%

<td style="text-align:left">National annual estimate<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">[167]</a></sup></td>
<td>The political status of Abkhazia is disputed. Having unilaterally declared independence from <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> in 1992, Abkhazia <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Abkhazia_and_South_Ossetia" title="International recognition of Abkhazia and South Ossetia">is formally recognised as an independent state</a> by 6 UN member states (one other state recognised it but then withdrew its recognition), while Georgia continues to claim it as part of its own territory, designating it as <a href="/wiki/Occupied_territories_of_Georgia" title="Occupied territories of Georgia">Russian-occupied territory</a>.
</td></tr>

<td style="text-align:right">53,532</td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-size:inherit"><span data-sort-value="6,996,671,398,429,415,000♠" style="display:none"></span>0.000671%
</td>
<td><span data-sort-value="000000002015-10-15-0000" style="white-space:nowrap">15 Oct 2015</span></td>
<td style="text-align:left">2015 census result<sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">[186]</a></sup></td>
<td><a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a>'s status is disputed. It  considers itself to be an independent state, but this is recognised by <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Abkhazia_and_South_Ossetia#States_formally_recognising_Abkhazia_or_South_Ossetia_as_independent" title="International recognition of Abkhazia and South Ossetia">only a  few other countries</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgian</a> government and most of the  world's other states consider South Ossetia <i><a href="/wiki/De_jure" title="De jure">de jure</a></i>  a part of Georgia's territory.
</td></tr>
